<script>
    function animateValue(obj, start = 0, end = null, duration = 1000) {
        if (obj) {

            var deci = false;
            var textStarting = obj.innerHTML;
            end = end || parseInt(textStarting.replace(/,/g, ''));
            var range = end - start;
            if (range &lt;= 30) {
                deci = true;
            }

            var minTimer = 50;
            var stepTime = Math.abs(Math.floor(duration / range));

            stepTime = Math.max(stepTime, minTimer);

            var startTime = new Date().getTime();
            var endTime = startTime + duration;
            var timer;

            function run() {
                var now = new Date().getTime();
                var remaining = Math.max((endTime - now) / duration, 0);
                var value = Math.round(end - (remaining * range));
                obj.innerHTML = textStarting.replace(/([0-9]+)/g, value);
                if (value === end) {
                    clearInterval(timer);
                    obj.innerHTML = textStarting.replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ",");
                }
            }

            timer = setInterval(run, stepTime);
            run();
        }
    }

    animateValue(document.getElementById('valueTot'));
    animateValue(document.getElementById('valueDed'));
    animateValue(document.getElementById('valueDedR'));
    animateValue(document.getElementById('valueRec'));
    animateValue(document.getElementById('valueRecR'));
    animateValue(document.getElementById('countriesR'));
  </script>

                });
                addTable();
                if ($(window).width() &lt; 1024 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &gt; 760) {
                    document.getElementById('new_confirmed').innerHTML = '&lt;i data-feather="trending-up"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;'
                    document.getElementById('new_dead').innerHTML = '&lt;i data-feather="trending-up"&gt;'
                    document.getElementById('new_recovered').innerHTML = '&lt;i data-feather="trending-up"&gt;'
                    document.getElementById('confirmed_col').innerHTML = "Cases"
                }

                feather.replace();

            });
        </script>

<script>
            $("#carouselButtons").children().on('click', function () {
                $("#carouselButtons").children().removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass('active');
            });
            $("#carouselExampleSlidesOnly").on("touchstart", function (event) {
                let xClick = event.originalEvent.touches[0].pageX;
                $(this).one("touchmove", function (event) {
                    let xMove = event.originalEvent.touches[0].pageX;
                    let index;
                    if (Math.floor(xClick - xMove) &gt; 9) {
                        $(this).carousel('next');
                        index = $(this).find('.active').index() + 1;
                        if (index &gt; 4) index = 0;

                    } else if (Math.floor(xClick - xMove) &lt; -9) {
                        $(this).carousel('prev');
                        index = $(this).find('.active').index() - 1;
                        if (index &lt; 0) index = 4;
                    } else {
                        return;
                    }
                    $("#carouselButtons").children().removeClass('active');
                    switch (index) {
                        case 0:
                            $("#overviewButton").addClass('active');
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            $("#tableButton").addClass('active');
                            break;
                        case 2:
                            $("#pieButton").addClass('active');
                            break;
                        case 3:
                            $("#lineButton").addClass('active');
                            break;
                        case 4:
                            $("#timeButton").addClass('active');
                            break;
                    }
                });
                $(".carousel").on("touchend", function () {
                    $(this).off("touchmove");
                });
            });
        </script>

        function getCookie(name) {
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
        }

        //Find the input search box
        let search = document.getElementById("searchChart");

        //Find every item inside the dropdown
        let items = document.getElementsByClassName("dropdown-item");

        function buildDropDown(values) {
            let contents = [];
            for (let name of values) {
                contents.push('&lt;option style="margin-left: 10px;" value="' + name + '"&gt;' + name + '&lt;/option&gt;');
            }
            $('#menuItems').append(contents.join(""));
        }
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $('#menuItems').selectpicker();
        });

        //Capture the event when user types into the search box
        window.addEventListener('input', function () {
            filter(search.value.trim().toLowerCase())
        });

        // For every word entered by the user, check if the symbol starts with that word
        // If it does show the symbol, else hide it
        function filter(word) {
            let length = items.length;
            let hidden = 0;
            for (let i = 0; i &lt; length; i++) {
                if (items[i].value.toLowerCase().startsWith(word)) {
                    $(items[i]).show()
                } else {
                    $(items[i]).hide();
                    hidden++
                }
            }

            // If all items are hidden, show the empty view
            if (hidden === length) {
                $('#empty').show()
            } else {
                $('#empty').hide()
            }
        }

        //If the user clicks on any item, set the title of the button as the text of the item
        $('#menuItems').on('click', '.dropdown-item', function () {
            $('#dropdown_search_region').text($(this)[0].value);
            $("#dropdown_search_region").dropdown('toggle');
            updateChart($(this)[0].value);
        });

        buildDropDown(names);

        // NOTIFICATION CODE
        var el = document.querySelector('.notification');

        if(getCookie('notifOpened') == null) {
            el.setAttribute('data-count', 1);
            el.classList.add('show-count');
        }

        function showLatestAdditions() {
            document.cookie = 'notifOpened=1';

            el.offsetWidth = el.offsetWidth;
            el.classList.remove('show-count');

            var collapsible = document.getElementById('notifs');
            if (collapsible.style.display === "block") {
                document.getElementById('notifTopBar').style.background = '#26b9b9';
                collapsible.style.display = "none";
            } else {
                collapsible.style.display = "block";
            }


        }
    </script>
<script>
        function timeSince(date) {
            let seconds = Math.floor((new Date() - date) / 1000);
            let interval = Math.floor(seconds / 31536000);
            if (interval &gt; 1) {
                return `Updated ${interval} years ago`;
            }
            interval = Math.floor(seconds / 2592000);
            if (interval &gt; 1) {
                return `Updated ${interval} months ago`;
            }
            interval = Math.floor(seconds / 86400);
            if (interval &gt; 1) {
                return `Updated ${interval} days ago`;
            }
            interval = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
            if (interval &gt; 1) {
                return `Updated ${interval} hours ago`;
            }
            interval = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
            if (interval &gt; 1) {
                return `Updated ${interval} minutes ago`;
            }
            return `Updated ${Math.floor(seconds)} seconds ago`;
        }
        document.getElementById("timestamp").innerHTML = timeSince(new Date(
            "2020-04-14T18:40:29.537859+00:00"));
    </script>

</script>
